✓ mjs.kotest.MarkdownTest ⇧

This is an example of using the description extension property, that can be used to describe the code being tested by a spec.

You can put limited Markdown in the description and it will be converted to HTML. Double newlines are converted into double line breaks.

- It converts code in backticks.

- It converts bold text.

- It converts italic text.

(It does not convert lists.)
